# JCE Cryptography Provider Architecture Audit

## Your Task

Audit the Java Cryptography Extension (JCE) provider architecture in OpenJDK. Find: 1. The file `src/java.base/share/classes/java/security/Provider.java` that defines the abstract `Provider` class and its inner `Service` class. 2. The file that defines `Security` class which manages registered providers (`src/java.base/share/classes/java/security/Security.java`). 3. The SunJCE provider implementation file (`src/java.crypto/share/classes/com/sun/crypto/provider/SunJCE.java` or under `java.base`). 4. The file that implements `Cipher.getInstance()` — the factory method that resolves providers (`src/java.base/share/classes/javax/crypto/Cipher.java`). 5. The `java.security` configuration file that lists default providers. Report each file path and key class/method.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/jdk--742e735d` (openjdk/jdk)

Perfect! I've completed the JCE Cryptography Provider Architecture audit for OpenJDK. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Files Found:

1. **Provider.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/java/security/Provider.java`)
   - Defines the abstract `Provider` class
   - Contains the inner `Service` class (starting at line 1500) which represents cryptographic services

2. **Security.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/java/security/Security.java`)
   - Central management class for registered providers
   - Loads configuration from `conf/security/java.security`
   - Provides `getProvider(name)` and `getProviders()` methods

3. **SunJCE.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/com/sun/crypto/provider/SunJCE.java`)
   - The SunJCE provider implementation extending Provider
   - Constructor at line 124 registers cryptographic algorithms via `putService()`
   - Supports RSA, DES, AES, Blowfish, HMAC, ChaCha20, and more

4. **Cipher.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/javax/crypto/Cipher.java`)
   - Three `getInstance()` factory method overloads:
     - Line 538: `getInstance(String transformation)`
     - Line 637: `getInstance(String transformation, String provider)`
     - Line 707: `getInstance(String transformation, Provider provider)`

5. **java.security** (`src/java.base/share/conf/security/java.security`)
   - Master configuration file listing providers with `security.provider.<n>=<providerName>`
   - Line 100 lists SunJCE as a default provider
   - Documents provider registration and preference ordering

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file paths, key symbols, and a detailed narrative explaining the JCE provider architecture and call chain.
